Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '5-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrixs and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_0 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing to defect is to maximize my own payoff. If I cooperate and all other players also cooperate, I will only receive a payoff of 5. However, if I defect while all other players cooperate, I will receive a payoff of 10. Even if some other players also defect, I will still receive a higher payoff of 8. Therefore, defecting gives me the best chance of maximizing my own payoff.
player_0 choose:  defect

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.

3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.

2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrixs and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_4 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing to defect is that I am solely focused on maximizing my own payoff. If I cooperate and the others also cooperate, I will only receive a payoff of 5. However, if I defect while the others cooperate, I will receive a higher payoff of 10. Additionally, if I cooperate and any of the other players defect, my payoff will be 0. Therefore, defecting seems to be the best strategy to maximize my own payoff in this situation.
player_4 choose:  defect

- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrixs and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_3 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing to defect is that I am solely focused on maximizing my own payoff. If I cooperate and the others also cooperate, I will only receive a payoff of 5. However, if I defect while the others cooperate, I will receive a higher payoff of 10. Additionally, if I cooperate and any of the other players defect, my payoff will be 0. Therefore, defecting seems to be the best strategy to ensure a higher payoff for myself.
player_3 choose:  defect

4. The others share the same payoff matrixs and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_2 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing 'defect' is that it maximizes my own payoff. If I choose to 'cooperate' and all other players also choose to 'cooperate', my payoff would be 5. However, if I choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', my payoff would be 10. Since my goal is to maximize my own payoff, it is in my best interest to choose 'defect'.
player_2 choose:  defect

2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrixs and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_2 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing to defect is to maximize my own payoff. If I cooperate and all other players also cooperate, my payoff would be 5. However, if I defect while all other players cooperate, my payoff would be 10. Since my goal is to maximize my own payoff, it is in my best interest to defect in this situation.
player_2 choose:  defect

- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrixs and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_1 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing to defect is that I am solely focused on maximizing my own payoff. By defecting, I have the potential to receive a payoff of 10 if all other players choose to cooperate. Even if some players choose to defect, I still have the opportunity to receive a higher payoff of 8 if I am one of the multiple players who defect while the others cooperate. This choice gives me the best chance of maximizing my own payoff, regardless of what the other players choose.
player_1 choose:  defect

- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrixs and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_1 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing 'defect' is to maximize my own payoff. If I choose to 'cooperate' and all other players also choose to 'cooperate', my payoff would be 5. However, if I choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', my payoff would be 10. By choosing 'defect', I have the potential to gain a higher payoff. Additionally, if I choose to 'cooperate' while any of the other players choose to 'defect', my payoff would be 0. Therefore, choosing 'defect' seems to be the rational choice in this situation.
player_1 choose:  defect

player_0 choose:  defect
Prompt: 
 Welcome to the '5-person Prisoner's Dilemma' game!

Here is what you need to know about the game:
1. As a player, you can choose from: 'cooperate', 'defect'.
2. Remember your goal is to maximize your own payoff. You should only care about your own interests.
3. Here is the payoff descriptions:
- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrixs and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_1 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing to defect is that by defecting, I have the potential to receive a higher payoff of 10 if all other players choose to cooperate. Even if some players choose to defect, I will still receive a payoff of 8 if I am one of the multiple players who defect while the others cooperate. This decision is based on the assumption that the other players are rational and will also choose to defect in order to maximize their own payoff.
player_1 choose:  defect

- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrixs and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_0 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing to defect is to maximize my own payoff. If I cooperate and all other players also cooperate, I will only receive a payoff of 5. However, if I defect while all other players cooperate, I will receive a payoff of 10. Additionally, if I cooperate while any other player defects, my payoff will be 0. Therefore, defecting seems to be the best strategy to ensure a higher payoff for myself.
player_0 choose:  defect

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_4 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing to defect is that I am solely focused on maximizing my own payoff. If I cooperate and the others also cooperate, I will only receive a payoff of 5. However, if I defect while the others cooperate, I will receive a higher payoff of 10. Additionally, if I cooperate and any of the other players defect, my payoff will be 0. Therefore, defecting seems to be the rational choice to maximize my own payoff in this game.
player_4 choose:  defect

My reason for choosing 'defect' is to maximize my own payoff. If I choose to 'cooperate' and all other players also choose to 'cooperate', my payoff would be 5. However, if I choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', my payoff would be 10. Since I should only care about my own interests in this game, it makes sense for me to choose the action that gives me the highest payoff.

- If only you choose to 'defect' while all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 10.
- If you and all other players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 5.
- If you and all other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 2.
- If you choose to 'cooperate' while any of other players choose to 'defect', your payoff is 0.
- If you are one of the m (m > 1) players who choose to 'defect' and while the other n (n>0) players choose to 'cooperate', your payoff is 8.
4. The others share the same payoff matrixs and goal with you. 

Please consider the information above and make your action.
Please give your action to choose, as well as the reasons.
player_3 choose:  I choose to 'defect'.

My reason for choosing to defect is to maximize my own payoff. If I cooperate and all other players also cooperate, I will only receive a payoff of 5. However, if I defect while all other players cooperate, I will receive a payoff of 10. Additionally, if I cooperate while any other player defects, my payoff will be 0. Therefore, defecting seems to be the rational choice to maximize my own payoff in this game.
player_3 choose:  defect
